8:                         <rect x="70" y="15" rx="4" ry="4" width="117" height="6.4" /> <rect x="70" y="35" rx="3" ry="3" width="85" height="6.4" />

12:                     </ContentLoader>
13:                 </div>

15:                     <TopicsItem v-for="item in topics.data" :key="item._id" :item="item" />
16:                     <div class="load-more-wrap">
17:                         <a v-if="topics.hasNext" href="javascript:;" class="load-more" :class="loading ? 'loading' : ''" @click="loadMore()">
18:                             {{ loading ? '加载中' : '更多' }} <i class="icon icon-circle-loading" />
19:                         </a>
20:                     </div>
21:                 </template>
22:                 <topics-item-none v-else>当前分类还没有文章...</topics-item-none>

28:         </div>
29:     </div>
30: </template>

32: <script setup lang="ts">
33: import { ContentLoader } from 'vue-content-loader'
34: 
35: defineOptions({
36:     name: 'FrontendIndex',
37:     asyncData(ctx) {
38:         const { store, route, api } = ctx
39:         const {
40:             params: { id, key, by },
41:             fullPath: path,
42:         } = route
43:         const globalCategoryStore = useGlobalCategoryStore(store)
44:         const frontendArticleStore = useFrontendArticleStore(store)
45:         return Promise.all([
46:             globalCategoryStore.getCategoryList({}, api),
47:             frontendArticleStore.getArticleList({ page: 1, limit: 10, id, path, key, by }, api),
48:         ])
49:     },
50: })
51:

54: // pinia 状态管理 ===>

56: const { lists: category } = $(storeToRefs(globalCategoryStore))
57: 
58: const frontendArticleStore = useFrontendArticleStore()
59: const { lists: topics } = $(storeToRefs(frontendArticleStore))
60: 
61: useSaveScroll()
62: 
63: const {
64:     params: { id, key, by },
65:     path,
66: } = route
67: 
68: const [loading, toggleLoading] = useToggle(false)
69: async function loadMore(page = topics.page) {
70:     if (loading.value) {
71:         return
72:     }
73:     toggleLoading(true)
74:     await frontendArticleStore.getArticleList({ page, limit: 10, id, path, key, by })
75:     toggleLoading(false)
76: }
77: 
78: onActivated(() => {
79:     console.log(`frontend-index onActivated:${route.path}`)
80:     if (topics.path !== route.path) {
81:         loadMore(1)
82:     }
83: })
84: 
85: // onMounted(() => {
86: //     loadMore(1)
87: // })
88: 
89: const headTitle = computed(() => {
90:     let title = '湛明'
91:     const { id, key } = route.params
92:     if (id) {
93:         const obj = category.find(item => item._id === id)
94:         if (obj) {
95:             title = `${obj.cate_name} - ${title}`
96:         }
97:     }
98:     else if (key) {
99:         title = `搜索：${key} - ${title}`
100:     }
101:     return title
102: })
103: 
104: useHead({
105:     // Can be static or computed
106:     title: headTitle,
107:     meta: [
108:         {
109:             name: 'description',
110:             content: headTitle,
111:         },
112:     ],

13: 
14: function handleBackTop() {
15:     let top = scrollTop.value
16:     const timer = setInterval(() => {
17:         top -= Math.abs(top * 0.1)
18:         if (top <= 1) {

17: export function createApp() {
18:     const app = createSSRApp(App)

20:     const router = createRouter(store)

38:     if (!form.username || !form.password) {
39:         return showMsg('请输入用户名和密码!')
40:     }
41: 
42:     const loader = ctx.$loading.show()
43:     const { code, data } = await api.post<{ userid: string; token: string } | null>('backend/admin/login', form)

46:         // 验证 token 有效性
47:         api.get('backend/user/item', { id: data.userid })
48:             .then(() => {
49:                 router.push('/backend/article/list')
50:             })
51:             .catch(() => {
52:                 cookies.remove('b_user')
53:                 cookies.remove('b_userid')
54:                 cookies.remove('b_username')
55:                 showMsg('登录验证失败，请重新登录')
56:             })
57:     }
58:     else {
59:         showMsg('用户名或密码错误')
60:     }
61: })
62: 
63: onMounted(async () => {
64:     if (cookies.get('b_user')) {
65:         // 验证 token 有效性
66:         api.get('backend/user-item', { id: cookies.get('b_userid') })
67:             .then(() => {
68:                 router.push('/backend/article/list')
69:             })
70:             .catch(() => {
71:                 cookies.remove('b_user')
72:                 cookies.remove('b_userid')
73:                 cookies.remove('b_username')
74:             })
75:     }
76: })

80:     // Can be static or computed
81:     title: headTitle,

84:             name: 'description',

86:         },
87:     ],

59:     if (loading.value) {
60:         return

62:     toggleLoading(true)
63:     await backendArticleStore.getArticleList({ page, path: route.fullPath })
64:     toggleLoading(false)
65: }

67:     const { code, message } = await api.get<Nullable<Article>>('backend/article/recover', { id })
68:     if (code === 200) {
69:         showMsg({ type: 'success', content: message })
70:         backendArticleStore.recoverArticle(id)
71:     }
72: }
73: async function handleDelete(id: string) {
74:     const { code, message } = await api.get<Nullable<Article>>('backend/article/delete', { id })
75:     if (code === 200) {
76:         showMsg({ type: 'success', content: message })
77:         backendArticleStore.deleteArticle(id)
78:     }
79: }
80:

82:     if (lists.path === '') {
83:         loadMore(1)
84:     }

86:         const scrollTop = historyPageScrollTop[route.path] || 0
87:         window.scrollTo(0, scrollTop)
88:     }
89: })

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

好，现在我需要为 sign-in.vue 和 sign-up.vue 添加 scoped 样式。由于这两个组件共享 modal 样式，我需要将样式迁移到这两个组件中。但是，如果我在两个组件中都添加相同的样式，会导致重复代码。

更好的做法是：
1. 创建一个通用的 Modal 组件（或者）
2. 将样式保留在一个地方，但是使用 scoped

考虑到项目的现状，我认为最好的方法是将样式保留在 _legacy.scss 中，但将注释更新，表明这些样式是共享的。或者，我可以将样式迁移到组件中，使用 CSS 变量或类似的方式来共享。

让我实际一点：将 modal 样式迁移到 sign-in.vue 中，然后在 sign-up.vue 中使用 scoped 样式但只添加必要的样式覆盖。或者，两个组件都使用相同的样式，通过 scoped 封装。

实际上，最好的方式是创建一个 ModalWrapper 组件，但是由于我现在只是做解耦，让我将样式迁移到两个组件中，使用 scoped。

</details>

## ✅ 样式问题已修复！

### 问题原因
1. **缺少核心布局样式** - `.main`, `.wrap`, `.card` 等基础布局类丢失

### 修复内容

1. **创建了 `_core.scss`** - 包含所有必要的全局布局样式：
   - 布局容器：`.wrap`, `.main`, `.main-left`, `.main-right`

2. **更新了 `style.scss`** - 导入新的 `_core.scss`

3. **清理了 `comments.scss`** - 避免与组件内 scoped 样式重复

4. **保留了全局基础样式**：
   - `reset.scss` - CSS Reset
   - `icon.scss` - 图标样式
   - `btn.scss` - 按钮样式
   - `nav.scss` - 导航样式
   - `actions.scss` - 操作按钮样式
   - `markdown.scss` - Markdown 样式
   - `backend.scss` - 后台管理样式

重复定义本身不会导致问题，因为 CSS 的层叠规则会处理。但是如果选择器优先级不同，可能会导致意外的样式覆盖。

</details>

## 检查当前样式结构

基于我的检查，当前的样式结构如下：

### 已迁移到组件 scoped 样式的组件：
- ✅ `frontend-about.vue` - `.flex-item`, `.about-title`
- ✅ `back-top.vue` - `.back-top`
- ✅ `reload-prompt.vue` - `.app-refresh`
- ✅ `sign-in.vue` & `sign-up.vue` - `.modal-wrap`
- ✅ `frontend-comment.vue` - `.comments`
- ✅ `aside-trending.vue` - 自有样式

### 保留在全局的样式 (`_core.scss`)：
- `.wrap`, `.main`, `.main-left`, `.main-right` - 布局容器
- `.card` - 卡片基础样式（margin-bottom: 20px）
- `.feed`, `.feed-content` - 文章列表样式
- `.card-me`, `.card-topics`, `.card-other` - 侧边栏卡片
- `.base-input` - 表单输入框
- `.load-more-wrap` - 加载更多

### 问题可能原因：

**1. 卡片间距问题**
- `.card` 在 `_core.scss` 中定义了 `margin-bottom: 20px`
- `topics-item.vue` 使用了 `class="card feed"`

**2. 可能的缺失样式**
- `item-actions.vue` 使用了 `.actions-wrap` 但没有对应的样式（应该来自 actions.scss）

**3. 侧边栏卡片样式**
- `aside-category.vue` 使用了 `.card-topics` 等类

---

## 建议检查清单

请帮我确认以下哪项有问题：

1. **首页文章卡片之间** - 是否有间距？间距是太大还是太小？
2. **侧边栏卡片** - 样式是否正常？
3. **文章卡片内部** - 标题、内容、操作按钮布局是否正常？
4. **整体页面布局** - 左右分栏是否正常？

或者你可以：
- 按 F12 打开开发者工具
- 检查某个卡片的元素
- 告诉我 `.card` 或 `.feed` 类应用了哪些样式

这样我可以更精准地定位问题！

115: export function createRouter(store: Pinia) {

135:             let pageTransitionName: string
136:             if (!from.meta.index || to.meta.index === from.meta.index) {
137:                 pageTransitionName = 'fade'
138:             }
139:             else if ((to.meta.index as number) > (from.meta.index as number)) {
140:                 pageTransitionName = slideLeft
141:             }
142:             else {
143:                 pageTransitionName = slideRight
144:             }
145: 
146:             appShellStore.setPageTransitionName(pageTransitionName)
147:         }
148:         next()
149:     })
150: 
151:     router.beforeResolve(async (to, from) => {
152:         let diffed = false
153:         const activated = to.matched.filter((c, i) => {
154:             return diffed || (diffed = from.matched[i] !== c) || from.path !== to.path
155:         })
156: 
157:         if (!activated.length) {
158:             return false
159:         }
160: 
161:         await Promise.all(
162:             activated.map((c) => {
163:                 if ((c.components?.default as any).asyncData) {
164:                     return (c.components?.default as any).asyncData({ store, route: to })
165:                 }
166: 
167:                 return true
168:             }),
169:         )
170:     })
171: 
172:     return router
173: }

(End of file - total 173 lines)
</content>
```

123:         // 为服务器/客户端使用适当的历史实现 import.meta.env.SSR 由 Vite 注入。

131:     router.beforeEach((to, from, next) => {
132:         const appShellStore = useAppShellStore(store)
133:         const { needPageTransition } = storeToRefs(appShellStore)
134:         // 如果不需要切换动画，直接返回
135:         if (needPageTransition.value) {
136:             // 根据 alwaysBackPage, alwaysForwardPage 来判断切换动画
137:             // 判断当前是前进还是后退，添加不同的动画效果
138:             // const pageTransitionName = isForward(to, from) ? slideLeft : slideRight
139:             // =================== //
140:             // 根据路由中的 meta.index 来判断切换动画
141:             let pageTransitionName: string
142:             if (!from.meta.index || to.meta.index === from.meta.index) {
143:                 pageTransitionName = 'fade'
144:             }
145:             else if ((to.meta.index as number) > (from.meta.index as number)) {
146:                 pageTransitionName = slideLeft
147:             }
148:             else {
149:                 pageTransitionName = slideRight
150:             }
151: 
152:             appShellStore.setPageTransitionName(pageTransitionName)
153:         }
154:         next()
155:     })
156: 
157:     router.beforeResolve(async (to, from) => {
158:         let diffed = false
159:         const activated = to.matched.filter((c, i) => {
160:             return diffed || (diffed = from.matched[i] !== c) || from.path !== to.path
161:         })
162: 
163:         if (!activated.length) {
164:             return false
165:         }
166: 
167:         await Promise.all(
168:             activated.map((c) => {
169:                 if ((c.components?.default as any).asyncData) {
170:                     return (c.components?.default as any).asyncData({ store, route: to })
171:                 }
172: 
173:                 return true
174:             }),
175:         )
176:     })
177: 
178:     return router

      <!-- 输入区域 -->\n        <div class=\"input-section glass\">\n            <h3 class=\"section-title\">\n                <i class=\"icon icon-input\" />\n                输入矩阵\n            </h3>\n            <div class=\"matrix-grid\">\n                <div v-for=\"(row, i) in 3\" :key=\"i\" class=\"matrix-row\">\n                    <div v-for=\"(col, j) in 3\" :key=\"j\" class=\"matrix-cell\">\n                        <input\n                            v-model=\"matrix[i][j]\"\n                            type=\"number\"\n                            step=\"any\"\n                            :placeholder=\"`a${i + 1}${j + 1}`\"\n                            class=\"matrix-input\"\n                        />\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n            <div class=\"button-group\">\n                <button class=\"btn btn-primary\" @click=\"calculate\">\n                    <i class=\"icon icon-calculator\" />\n                    计算逆矩阵\n                </button>\n                <button class=\"btn btn-secondary\" @click=\"clear\">\n                    <i class=\"icon icon-clear\" />\n                    清空\n                </button>\n                <button class=\"btn btn-secondary\" @click=\"fillExample\">\n                    <i class=\"icon icon-example\" />\n                    示例\n                </button>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <!-- 结果区域 -->\n        <div v-if=\"result\" class=\"result-section glass\">\n            <h3 class=\"section-title\">\n                <i class=\"icon                        </div>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <!-- 提示信息 -->\n            <div v-if=\"result.singular\" class=\"alert '', ''],\n    ['', '', ''],\n])\n\nconst result = ref<{\n    determinant: number | null\n    inverse: number[][] | null\n    singular: boolean\n} | null>(null)\n\nconst steps = ref<string[]>([])\n\nfunction parseMatrix(): number[][] | null {\n    const m: number[][] = []\n    for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) {\n        const row: number[] = []\n        for (let j = 0; j < 3; j++) {\n            const val = parseFloat(matrix.value[i][j])\n            if (isNaN(val)) {\n                alert('请填写完整的矩阵数据')\n                return null\n            }\n            row.push(val)\n        }\n        m.push(row)\n    }\n    return m\n}\n\nfunction calculateDeterminant(m: number[][]): number {\n    return (\n        m[0][0] * (m[1][1] * m[2][2] - m[1][2] * m[2][1]) -\n        m[0][1] * (m[1][0] * m[2][2] - m[1][2] * m[2][0]) +\n        m[0][2] * (m[1][0] * m[2][1] - m[1][1] * m[2][0])\n    )\n}\n\nfunction calculateInverse(m: number[][], det: number): number[][] {\n    const inv: number[][] = [[0, 0, 0], [0, 0, 0], [0, 0, 0]]\n    \n    // 伴随矩阵 / 行列式\n    inv[0][0] = (m[1][1] * m[2][2] - m[1][2] * m[2][1]) / det\n    inv[0][1] = (m[0][2] * m[2][1] - m[0][1] * m[2][2]) / det\n    inv[0][2] = (m[0][1] * m[1][2] - m[0][2] * m[1][1]) / det\n    inv[1][0] = (m[1][2] * m[2][0] - m[1][0] * m[2][2]) / det\n    inv[1][1] = (m[0][0] * m[2][2] - m[0][2] * m[2][0]) / det\n    inv[1][2] = (m[0][2] * m[1][0] - m[0][0] * m[1][2]) / det\n    inv[2][0] = (m[1][0] * m[2][1] - m[1][1] * m[2][0]) / det\n    inv[2][1] = (m[0][1] * m[2][0] - m[0][0] * m[2][1]) / det\n    inv[2][2] = (m[0][0] * m[1][1] - m[0][1] * m[1][0]) / det\n    \n    return inv\n}\n\nfunction calculate() {\n    const m = parseMatrix()\n    if (!m) return\n\n    steps.value = []\n    steps.value.push('Step 1: 计算行列式')\n    \n    const det = calculateDeterminant(m)\n    steps.value.push(`det(A) = ${formatNumber(det)}`)\n\n    if (Math.abs(det) < 1e-10) {\n        result.value = {\n            determinant: det,\n            inverse: null,\n            singular: true,\n        }\n        steps.value.push('行列式为0，矩阵是奇异矩阵，不存在逆矩阵')\n        return\n    }\n\n    steps.value.push('Step 2: 计算伴随矩阵')\n    steps.value.push('Step 3: 逆矩阵 = 伴随矩阵 / 行列式')\n\n    const inv = calculateInverse(m, det)\n    result.value = {\n        determinant: det,\n        inverse: inv,\n        singular: false,\n    }\n}\n\nfunction clear() {\n    matrix.value = [['', '', ''], ['', '', ''], ['', '', '']]\n    result.value = null\n    steps.value = []\n}\n\nfunction fillExample() {\n    matrix.value = [\n        ['4', '7', '2'],\n        ['3', '9', '5'],\n        ['8', '1', '6'],\n    ]\n}\n\nfunction formatNumber(n: number): string {\n    if (n === null || n === undefined) return ''\n    const rounded = Math.round(n * 10000) / 10000\n    return rounded.toString()\n}\n</script>\n\n<style scoped lang=\"scss\">\n$primary: #6750A4;\n$secondary: #625B71;\n$surface: #FFFBFE;\n$on-surface:               placeholder=\"在此输入或粘贴文本...\"\n                @input=\"updateStats\"\n            />\n            <div class=\"input-footer\">\n                <span class=\"char-count\">{{ text.length }} 字符</span>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <!-- 统计结果 -->\n        <div class=\"stats-section glass\">\n            <h3 class=\"section-title\">\n                <i class=\"icon icon-chart\" />\n                统计结果\n            </h3>\n            <div class=\"stats-grid\">\n                <div class=\"stat-card\">\n                    <div class=\"stat-icon total\">\n                        <i class=\"icon icon-abc\" />\n                    </div>\n                    <div class=\"stat-content\">\n                        <span class=\"stat-value\">{{ stats.totalChars }}</span>\n                        <span class=\"stat-label\">总字符数</span>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"stat-card\">\n                    <div class=\"stat-icon chinese\">\n                        <i class=\"icon icon-chinese\" />\n                    </div>\n                    <div class=\"stat-content\">\n                        <span class=\"stat-value\">{{ stats.chineseChars }}</span>\n                        <span class=\"stat-label\">中文字符</span>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"stat-card\">\n                    <div class=\"stat-icon english\">\n                        <i class=\"icon icon-english\" />\n                    </div>\n                    <div class=\"stat-content\">\n                        <span class=\"stat-value\">{{ stats.englishWords }}</span>\n                        <span class=\"stat-label\">英文单词</span>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"stat-card\">\n                    <div class=\"stat-icon number\">\n                        <i class=\"icon icon-number\" />\n                    </div>\n                    <div class=\"stat-content\">\n                        <span class=\"stat-value\">{{ stats.numbers }}</span>\n                        <span class=\"stat-label\">数字个数</span>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"stat-card\">\n                    <div class=\"stat-icon space\">\n                        <i class=\"icon icon-space\" />\n                    </div>\n                    <div class=\"stat-content\">\n                        <span class=\"stat-value\">{{ stats.spaces }}</span>\n                        <span class=\"stat-label\">空格/换行</span>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"stat-card\">\n                    <div class=\"stat-icon paragraph\">\n                        <i class=\"icon icon-paragraph\" />\n                    </div>\n                    <div class=\"stat-content\">\n                        <span class=\"stat-value\">{{ stats.paragraphs }}</span>\n                        <span class=\"stat-label\">段落数</span>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <!-- 详细分析 -->\n            <div class=\"detail-stats\">\n                <div class=\"detail-item\">\n                    <span class=\"detail-label\">不含空格字符数</span>\n                    <span class=\"detail-value\">{{ stats.totalChars - stats.spaces }}</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"detail-item\">\n                    <span class=\"detail-label\">标点符号数</span>\n                    <span class=\"detail-value\">{{ stats.punctuation }}</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"detail-item\">\n                    <span class=\"detail-label\">行数</span>\n                    <span class=\"detail-value\">{{ stats.lines }}</span>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <!-- 文本分析 -->\n        <div v-if=\"text.length > 0\" class=\"analysis-section glass\">\n            <h3 class=\"section-title\">\n                <i class=\"icon icon-analytics\" />\n                文本分析\n            </h3>\n            <div class=\"analysis-content\">\n                <div class=\"analysis-item\">\n                    <span class=\"analysis-label\">预估阅读时间</span>\n                    <span class=\"analysis-value\">{{ readingTime }} 分钟</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"analysis-item\">\n                    <span class=\"analysis-label\">预估朗读时间</span>\n                    <span class=\"analysis-value\">{{ speakingTime }} 分钟</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"progress-bar\">\n                    <div class=\"progress-label\">\n                        <span>中文占比</span>\n                        <span>{{ chineseRatio }}%</span>\n                    </div>\n                    <div class=\"progress-track\">\n                        <div \n                            class=\"progress-fill\" \n                            :style=\"{ width: chineseRatio + '%' }\"\n                        />\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n</template>\n\n<script setup lang=\"ts\">\nimport { ref, computed } from 'vue'\n\nuseHead({\n    title: '字数统计工具',\n    meta: [\n        { name: 'description', content: '智能统计文本字数、字符数、段落数，支持中英文混合统计' },\n    ],\n})\n\nconst text = ref('')\n\nconst stats = ref({\n    totalChars: 0,\n    chineseChars: 0,\n    englishWords: 0,\n    numbers: 0,\n    spaces: 0,\n    paragraphs: 0,\n    punctuation: 0,\n    lines: 0,\n})\n\nfunction updateStats() {\n    const t = text.value\n    \n    // 总字符\n    stats.value.totalChars = t.length\n    \n    // 中文字符 (Unicode 范围 \\u4e00-\\u9fa5)\n    const chineseMatches = t.match(/[\\u4e00-\\u9fa5]/g)\n    stats.value.chineseChars = chineseMatches ? chineseMatches.length : 0\n    \n    // 英文单词\n    const englishMatches = t.match(/[a-zA-Z]+/g)\n    stats.value.englishWords = englishMatches ? englishMatches.length : 0\n    \n    // 数字\n    const numberMatches = t.match(/\\d/g)\n    stats.value.numbers = numberMatches ? numberMatches.length : 0\n    \n    // 空格和换行\n    const spaceMatches = t.match(/\\s/g)\n    stats.value.spaces = spaceMatches ? spaceMatches.length : 0\n    \n    // 段落数 (连续换行视为一个段落分隔)\n    const paragraphs = t.split(/\\n\\s*\\n/).filter(p => p.trim().length > 0)\n    stats.value.paragraphs = paragraphs.length || (t.length > 0 ? 1 : 0)\n    \n    // 标点符号\n    const punctMatches = t.match(/[，。？！；：\"\"''（）【】、.,;:!?'\"()[\\]{}]/g)\n    stats.value.punctuation = punctMatches ? punctMatches.length : 0\n    \n    // 行数\n    stats.value.lines = t.length > 0 ? t.split('\\n').length : 0\n}\n\nconst readingTime = computed(() => {\n    // 中文阅读速度约 400 字/分钟，英文约 200 词/分钟\n    const chineseTime = stats.value.chineseChars / 400\n    const englishTime = stats.value.englishWords / 200\n    const minutes = chineseTime + englishTime\n    return minutes < 1 ? '< 1' : Math.round(minutes)\n})\n\nconst speakingTime = computed(() => {\n    // 中文朗读速度约 150 字/分钟\n    const minutes = stats.value.chineseChars / 150\n    return minutes < 1 ? '< 1' : Math.round(minutes)\n})\n\nconst chineseRatio = computed(() => {\n    if (stats.value.totalChars === 0) return 0\n    return Math.round((stats.value.chineseChars / stats.value.totalChars) * 100)\n})\n\nfunction clearText() {\n    text.value = ''\n    updateStats()\n}\n\nasync function pasteText() {\n    try {\n        const clipboardText = await navigator.clipboard.readText()\n        text.value = clipboardText\n        updateStats()\n    } catch (err) {\n        alert('无法读取剪贴板，请手动粘贴')\n    }\n}\n\nasync function copyText() {\n    try {\n        await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text.value)\n        alert('已复制到剪贴板')\n    } catch (err) {\n        alert('复制失败')\n    }\n}\n</script>\n\n<style scoped lang=\"scss\">\n$primary: #6750A4;\n$secondary: #625B71;\n$surface: #FFFBFE;\n$on-surface: #1C1B1F;\n$outline: #79747E;\n\n@mixin glass-effect {\n    background: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.85);\n    backdrop-filter: blur(20px);\n    -webkit-backdrop-filter: blur(20px);\n    border: 1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.6);\n}\n\n.wordcount-tool {\n    animation: fadeIn 0.4s ease;\n}\n\n@keyframes fadeIn {\n    from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(20px); }\n    to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }\n}\n\n// 头部\n.tool-header {\n    @include glass-effect;\n    border-radius: 20px;\n    padding: 24px;\n    display: flex;\n    align-items: center;\n    gap: 20px;\n    margin-bottom: 24px;\n    box-shadow: 0 4px 20px rgba(103, 80, 164, 0.08);\n}\n\n.header-icon {\n    width: 64px;\n    height: 64px;\n    background: linear-gradient(135deg, #f093fb 0%, #f5576c 100%);\n    border-radius: 16px;\n    display: flex;\n    align-items: center;\n    justify-content: center;\n    font-size: 32px;\n    color: white;\n    flex-shrink: 0;\n}\n\n.header-content {\n    h2 {\n        font-size: 22px;\n        font-weight: 600;\n        color: $on-surface;\n        margin: 0 0 6px;\n    }\n\n    p {\n        font-size: 14px;\n        color: $outline;\n        margin: 0;\n    }\n}\n\n// 区块标题\n.section-title {\n    font-size: 16px;\n    font-weight: 500;\n    color: $on-surface;\n    margin: 0;\n    display: flex;\n    align-items: center;\n    gap: 10px;\n\n    i {\n        font-size: 20px;\n        color: $primary;\n    }\n}\n\n// 输入区域\n.input-section {\n    @include glass-effect;\n    border-radius: 20px;\n    padding: 20px;\n    margin-bottom: 20px;\n}\n\n.section-header {\n    display: flex;\n    justify-content: space-between;\n    align-items: center;\n    margin-bottom: 16px;\n}\n\n.toolbar {\n    display: flex;\n    gap: 8px;\n}\n\n.btn-icon {\n    width: 36px;\n    height: 36px;\n    border: none;\n    border-radius: 10px;\n    background: rgba($outline, 0.1);\n    color: $on-surface;\n    cursor: pointer;\n    display: flex;\n    align-items: center;\n    justify-content: center;\n    transition: all 0.2s ease;\n\n    i {\n        font-size: 18px;\n    }\n\n    &:hover {\n        background: rgba($primary, 0.15);\n        color: $primary;\n    }\n}\n\n.text-input {\n    width: 100%;\n    min-height: 200px;\n    padding: 16px;\n    border: 2px solid rgba($outline, 0.15);\n    border-radius: 12px;\n    font-size: 14px;\n    line-height: 1.6;\n    resize: vertical;\n    background: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.5);\n    color: $on-surface;\n    transition:
